    (function () {
      function isLocalStorageNameSupported() {
        const testKey = 'test';
        const storage = window.localStorage;
        try {
          storage.setItem(testKey, '1');
          storage.removeItem(testKey);
          return true;
        } catch (error) {
          return false;
        }
      }
      // 优先级提高到所有静态资源的前面，语言不对，加载其他静态资源没意义
      const pathname = location.pathname;

      function isZhCN(pathname) {
        return /-cn\/?$/.test(pathname);
      }
      function getLocalizedPathname(path, zhCN) {
        const pathname = path.indexOf('/') === 0 ? path : '/' + path;
        if (!zhCN) {
          // to enUS
          return /\/?index(-cn)?/.test(pathname) ? '/' : pathname.replace('-cn', '');
        } else if (pathname === '/') {
          return '/index-cn';
        } else if (pathname.indexOf('/') === pathname.length - 1) {
          return pathname.replace(/\/$/, '-cn/');
        }
        return pathname + '-cn';
      }

      // 兼容旧的 URL， `?locale=...`
      const queryString = location.search;
      if (queryString) {
        const isZhCNConfig = queryString.indexOf('zh-CN') > -1;
        if (isZhCNConfig && !isZhCN(pathname)) {
          location.pathname = getLocalizedPathname(pathname, isZhCNConfig);
        }
      }

      // 首页无视链接里面的语言设置 https://github.com/ant-design/ant-design/issues/4552
      if (isLocalStorageNameSupported() && (pathname === '/' || pathname === '/index-cn')) {
        const lang =
          (window.localStorage && localStorage.getItem('locale')) ||
          ((navigator.language || navigator.browserLanguage).toLowerCase() === 'zh-cn'
            ? 'zh-CN'
            : 'en-US');
        // safari is 'zh-cn', while other browser is 'zh-CN';
        if ((lang === 'zh-CN') !== isZhCN(pathname)) {
          location.pathname = getLocalizedPathname(pathname, lang === 'zh-CN');
        }
      }
      document.documentElement.className += isZhCN(pathname) ? 'zh-cn' : 'en-us';
    })();

icon-link"></span></a>2.0.0</h2><p><code>2025-11-22</code></p><p>🏆 Ant Design X 2.0.0 has been released!</p><p><code>@ant-design/x</code> - Smart UI Construction Framework</p><p>A React UI library based on the Ant Design system, specifically designed for AI-driven interfaces. It includes ready-to-use intelligent chat components and seamless integration with API services, enabling rapid development of smart application interfaces.</p><p><code>@ant-design/x-markdown</code> - High-performance streaming rendering engine</p><p>A Markdown rendering solution optimized for streaming content, featuring robust extensibility and exceptional performance with support for formulas, code highlighting, Mermaid diagrams, and more, ensuring a seamless content display experience.</p><p><code>@ant-design/x-sdk</code> - AI Chat Data Flow Management</p><p>Provide a complete set of tool APIs, out-of-the-box AI chat application data flow management, simplify development processes, and enhance development efficiency.</p><h5 id="upgrade-required"><a aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#upgrade-required"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Upgrade Required</h5><p>🌟 We have prepared an upgrade guide. icon-link"></span></a>1.0.0</h2><p><code>2024-11-22</code></p><p>🎉 We are thrilled to announce the official release of <a href="https://x.ant.design">Ant Design X</a> 1.0.0!</p><ul><li>🌈 <strong>Derived from Best Practices of Enterprise-Level AI Products</strong>: Built on the RICH interaction paradigm, delivering an exceptional AI interaction experience.</li><li>🧩 <strong>Flexible and Diverse Atomic Components</strong>: Covers most AI dialogue scenarios, empowering you to quickly build personalized AI interaction interfaces.</li><li>⚡ <strong>Out-of-the-Box Model Integration</strong>: Easily connect with inference services compatible with OpenAI standards.</li><li>🔄 <strong>Efficient Management of Conversation Data Flows</strong>: Provides powerful tools for managing data flows, enhancing development efficiency.</li><li>📦 <strong>Rich Template Support</strong>: Offers multiple templates for quickly starting LUI application development.</li><li>🛡 <strong>Complete TypeScript Support</strong>: Developed with TypeScript, ensuring robust type coverage to improve the development experience and reliability.</li><li>🎨 <strong>Advanced Theme Customization</strong>: Supports fine-grained style adjustments to meet diverse use cases and personalization needs.</li></ul><h2 id="100-alpha12"><a aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"
